<s> his wife was always out when she was in town and his daughter would flibberty gibbet all over the place like most young women since the war <\s>
<s> still he must be thankful that she had been too young to do anything in that war itself <\s>
<s> not of course that he had not supported the war from its inception with all his soul but between that and supporting it with the bodies of his wife and daughter there had been a gap fixed by something old fashioned within him which abhorred emotional extravagance <\s>
<s> he had for instance strongly objected to annette so attractive and in 1914 only thirty four going to her native france her chere patrie as under the stimulus of war she had begun to call it to nurse her braves poilus forsooth <\s>
<s> ruining her health and her looks <\s>
<s> as if she were really a nurse <\s>
<s> he had put a stopper on it <\s>
<s> let her do needlework for them at home or knit <\s>
<s> she had not gone therefore and had never been quite the same woman since <\s>
<s> a bad tendency of hers to mock at him not openly but in continual little ways had grown <\s>
<s> as for fleur the war had resolved the vexed problem whether or not she should go to school <\s>
<s> she was better away from her mother in her war mood from the chance of air raids and the impetus to do extravagant things so he had placed her in a seminary as far west as had seemed to him compatible with excellence and had missed her horribly <\s>
<s> he had never regretted the somewhat outlandish name by which at her birth he had decided so suddenly to call her marked concession though it had been to the french <\s>
<s> a pretty name a pretty child <\s>
<s> but restless too restless and wilful <\s>
<s> knowing her power too over her father <\s>
<s> soames often reflected on the mistake it was to dote on his daughter <\s>
<s> to get old and dote <\s>
<s> he was getting on but he didn't feel it for fortunately perhaps considering annette's youth and good looks his second marriage had turned out a cool affair <\s>
<s> he had known but one real passion in his life for that first wife of his irene <\s>
<s> yes and that fellow his cousin jolyon who had gone off with her was looking very shaky they said <\s>
<s> no wonder at seventy two after twenty years of a third marriage <\s>
<s> soames paused a moment in his march to lean over the railings of the row <\s>
<s> a suitable spot for reminiscence half way between that house in park lane which had seen his birth and his parents deaths and the little house in montpellier square where thirty five years ago he had enjoyed his first edition of matrimony <\s>
<s> now after twenty years of his second edition that old tragedy seemed to him like a previous existence which had ended when fleur was born in place of the son he had hoped for <\s>
<s> for many years he had ceased regretting even vaguely the son who had not been born fleur filled the bill in his heart <\s>
<s> after all she bore his name and he was not looking forward at all to the time when she would change it <\s>
<s> indeed if he ever thought of such a calamity it was seasoned by the vague feeling that he could make her rich enough to purchase perhaps and extinguish the name of the fellow who married her why not since as it seemed women were equal to men nowadays <\s>
<s> and soames secretly convinced that they were not passed his curved hand over his face vigorously till it reached the comfort of his chin <\s>
<s> thanks to abstemious habits he had not grown fat and gabby his nose was pale and thin his grey moustache close clipped his eyesight unimpaired <\s>
<s> a slight stoop closened and corrected the expansion given to his face by the heightening of his forehead in the recession of his grey hair <\s>
<s> little change had time wrought in the warmest of the young forsytes as the last of the old forsytes timothy now in his hundred and first year would have phrased it <\s>
<s> the shade from the plane trees fell on his neat homburg hat he had given up top hats it was no use attracting attention to wealth in days like these <\s>
<s> his thoughts travelled sharply to madrid the easter before the war when having to make up his mind about that goya picture he had taken a voyage of discovery to study the painter on his spot <\s>
<s> the fellow had impressed him great range real genius <\s>
<s> highly as the chap ranked he would rank even higher before they had finished with him <\s>
<s> the second goya craze would be greater even than the first oh yes <\s>
<s> and he had bought <\s>
<s> on that visit he had as never before commissioned a copy of a fresco painting called la vendimia wherein was the figure of a girl with an arm akimbo who had reminded him of his daughter <\s>
<s> he had it now in the gallery at mapledurham and rather poor it was you couldn't copy goya <\s>
<s> he would still look at it however if his daughter were not there for the sake of something irresistibly reminiscent in the light erect balance of the figure the width between the arching eyebrows the eager dreaming of the dark eyes <\s>
<s> curious that fleur should have dark eyes when his own were grey no pure forsyte had brown eyes and her mother's blue <\s>
<s> but of course her grandmother lamotte's eyes were dark as treacle <\s>
<s> he began to walk on again toward hyde park corner <\s>
<s> no greater change in all england than in the row <\s>
<s> born almost within hail of it he could remember it from 1860 on <\s>
<s> brought there as a child between the crinolines to stare at tight trousered dandies in whiskers riding with a cavalry seat to watch the doffing of curly brimmed and white top hats the leisurely air of it all and the little bow legged man in a long red waistcoat who used to come among the fashion with dogs on several strings and try to sell one to his mother king charles spaniels italian greyhounds affectionate to her crinoline you never saw them now <\s>
<s> you saw no quality of any sort indeed just working people sitting in dull rows with nothing to stare at but a few young bouncing females in pot hats riding astride or desultory colonials charging up and down on dismal looking hacks with here and there little girls on ponies or old gentlemen jogging their livers or an orderly trying a great galumphing cavalry horse no thoroughbreds no grooms no bowing no scraping no gossip nothing only the trees the same the trees indifferent to the generations and declensions of mankind <\s>
<s> a democratic england dishevelled hurried noisy and seemingly without an apex <\s>
<s> and that something fastidious in the soul of soames turned over within him <\s>
<s> gone forever the close borough of rank and polish <\s>
<s> wealth there was oh yes <\s>
<s> wealth he himself was a richer man than his father had ever been but manners flavour quality all gone engulfed in one vast ugly shoulder rubbing petrol smelling cheerio <\s>
<s> little half beaten pockets of gentility and caste lurking here and there dispersed and chetif as annette would say but nothing ever again firm and coherent to look up to <\s>
<s> and into this new hurly burly of bad manners and loose morals his daughter flower of his life was flung <\s>
<s> and when those labour chaps got power if they ever did the worst was yet to come <\s>
<s> he passed out under the archway at last no longer thank goodness disfigured by the gungrey of its search light <\s>
<s> they'd better put a search light on to where they're all going he thought and light up their precious democracy <\s>
<s> and he directed his steps along the club fronts of piccadilly <\s>
<s> george forsyte of course would be sitting in the bay window of the iseeum <\s>
<s> the chap was so big now that he was there nearly all his time like some immovable sardonic humorous eye noting the decline of men and things <\s>
<s> and soames hurried ever constitutionally uneasy beneath his cousin's glance <\s>
<s> george who as he had heard had written a letter signed patriot in the middle of the war complaining of the government's hysteria in docking the oats of race horses <\s>
<s> yes there he was tall ponderous neat clean shaven with his smooth hair hardly thinned smelling no doubt of the best hair wash and a pink paper in his hand <\s>
<s> well he didn't change <\s>
<s> and for perhaps the first time in his life soames felt a kind of sympathy tapping in his waistcoat for that sardonic kinsman <\s>
<s> with his weight his perfectly parted hair and bull like gaze he was a guarantee that the old order would take some shifting yet <\s>
<s> he saw george move the pink paper as if inviting him to ascend the chap must want to ask something about his property <\s>
<s> it was still under soames control for in the adoption of a sleeping partnership at that painful period twenty years back when he had divorced irene soames had found himself almost insensibly retaining control of all purely forsyte affairs <\s>
<s> hesitating for just a moment he nodded and went in <\s>
<s> since the death of his brother in law montague dartie in paris which no one had quite known what to make of except that it was certainly not suicide the iseeum club had seemed more respectable to soames <\s>
<s> george too he knew had sown the last of his wild oats and was committed definitely to the joys of the table eating only of the very best so as to keep his weight down and owning as he said just one or two old screws to give me an interest in life <\s>
<s> he joined his cousin therefore in the bay window without the embarrassing sense of indiscretion he had been used to feel up there <\s>
<s> george put out a well kept hand <\s>
<s> haven't seen you since the war he said <\s>
<s> thanks said soames coldly well enough <\s>

<s> he's a rum customer <\s>
<s> what did you want to see me about <\s>
<s> old timothy he might go off the hooks at any moment <\s>

<s> he ought to have a pyramid by rights <\s>
<s> soames shook his head <\s>
<s> highgate the family vault <\s>
<s> well i suppose the old girls would miss him if he was anywhere else <\s>
<s> they say he still takes an interest in food <\s>
<s> he might last on you know <\s>

<s> and he directed his steps along the club fronts of piccadilly <\s>
<s> george forsyte of course would be sitting in the bay window of the iseeum <\s>
<s> the chap was so big now that he was there nearly all his time like some immovable sardonic humorous eye noting the decline of men and things <\s>
<s> and soames hurried ever constitutionally uneasy beneath his cousin's glance <\s>
<s> george who as he had heard had written a letter signed patriot in the middle of the war complaining of the government's hysteria in docking the oats of race horses <\s>
<s> yes there he was tall ponderous neat clean shaven with his smooth hair hardly thinned smelling no doubt of the best hair wash and a pink paper in his hand <\s>
<s> well he didn't change <\s>
<s> and for perhaps the first time in his life soames felt a kind of sympathy tapping in his waistcoat for that sardonic kinsman <\s>
<s> with his weight his perfectly parted hair and bull like gaze he was a guarantee that the old order would take some shifting yet <\s>
<s> he saw george move the pink paper as if inviting him to ascend the chap must want to ask something about his property <\s>
<s> it was still under soames control for in the adoption of a sleeping partnership at that painful period twenty years back when he had divorced irene soames had found himself almost insensibly retaining control of all purely forsyte affairs <\s>
<s> hesitating for just a moment he nodded and went in <\s>
<s> since the death of his brother in law montague dartie in paris which no one had quite known what to make of except that it was certainly not suicide the iseeum club had seemed more respectable to soames <\s>
<s> george too he knew had sown the last of his wild oats and was committed definitely to the joys of the table eating only of the very best so as to keep his weight down and owning as he said just one or two old screws to give me an interest in life <\s>
<s> he joined his cousin therefore in the bay window without the embarrassing sense of indiscretion he had been used to feel up there <\s>
<s> george put out a well kept hand <\s>
<s> haven't seen you since the war he said <\s>
<s> thanks said soames coldly well enough <\s>
<s> some hidden jest curved for a moment george's fleshy face and gloated from his eye <\s>
<s> that belgian chap profond he said is a member here now <\s>
<s> he's a rum customer <\s>
<s> what did you want to see me about <\s>
<s> old timothy he might go off the hooks at any moment <\s>

<s> soames shook his head <\s>
<s> highgate the family vault <\s>
<s> well i suppose the old girls would miss him if he was anywhere else <\s>
<s> they say he still takes an interest in food <\s>
<s> he might last on you know <\s>
<s> don't we get anything for the old forsytes <\s>
<s> ten of them average age eighty eight i worked it out <\s>
<s> that ought to be equal to triplets <\s>
<s> said soames i must be getting on <\s>
<s> you unsociable devil george's eyes seemed to answer <\s>
<s> yes that's all look him up in his mausoleum the old chap might want to prophesy <\s>
<s> the grin died on the rich curves of his face and he added haven't you attorneys invented a way yet of dodging this damned income tax <\s>
<s> it hits the fixed inherited income like the very deuce <\s>
<s> i used to have two thousand five hundred a year now i've got a beggarly fifteen hundred and the price of living doubled <\s>
<s> his wife was always out when she was in town and his daughter would flibberty gibbet all over the place like most young women since the war <\s>
<s> still he must be thankful that she had been too young to do anything in that war itself <\s>
<s> not of course that he had not supported the war from its inception with all his soul but between that and supporting it with the bodies of his wife and daughter there had been a gap fixed by something old fashioned within him which abhorred emotional extravagance <\s>
<s> he had for instance strongly objected to annette so attractive and in 1914 only thirty four going to her native france her chere patrie as under the stimulus of war she had begun to call it to nurse her braves poilus forsooth <\s>
<s> ruining her health and her looks <\s>
<s> as if she were really a nurse <\s>
<s> he had put a stopper on it <\s>
<s> let her do needlework for them at home or knit <\s>
<s> she had not gone therefore and had never been quite the same woman since <\s>
<s> a bad tendency of hers to mock at him not openly but in continual little ways had grown <\s>
<s> as for fleur the war had resolved the vexed problem whether or not she should go to school <\s>
<s> she was better away from her mother in her war mood from the chance of air raids and the impetus to do extravagant things so he had placed her in a seminary as far west as had seemed to him compatible with excellence and had missed her horribly <\s>
<s> he had never regretted the somewhat outlandish name by which at her birth he had decided so suddenly to call her marked concession though it had been to the french <\s>
<s> a pretty name a pretty child <\s>
<s> but restless too restless and wilful <\s>
<s> knowing her power too over her father <\s>
<s> soames often reflected on the mistake it was to dote on his daughter <\s>
<s> to get old and dote <\s>
<s> he was getting on but he didn't feel it for fortunately perhaps considering annette's youth and good looks his second marriage had turned out a cool affair <\s>
<s> he had known but one real passion in his life for that first wife of his irene <\s>
<s> yes and that fellow his cousin jolyon who had gone off with her was looking very shaky they said <\s>
<s> no wonder at seventy two after twenty years of a third marriage <\s>
<s> soames paused a moment in his march to lean over the railings of the row <\s>
<s> a suitable spot for reminiscence half way between that house in park lane which had seen his birth and his parents deaths and the little house in montpellier square where thirty five years ago he had enjoyed his first edition of matrimony <\s>
<s> now after twenty years of his second edition that old tragedy seemed to him like a previous existence which had ended when fleur was born in place of the son he had hoped for <\s>
<s> for many years he had ceased regretting even vaguely the son who had not been born fleur filled the bill in his heart <\s>
<s> after all she bore his name and he was not looking forward at all to the time when she would change it <\s>
<s> indeed if he ever thought of such a calamity it was seasoned by the vague feeling that he could make her rich enough to purchase perhaps and extinguish the name of the fellow who married her why not since as it seemed women were equal to men nowadays <\s>
<s> and soames secretly convinced that they were not passed his curved hand over his face vigorously till it reached the comfort of his chin <\s>
<s> thanks to abstemious habits he had not grown fat and gabby his nose was pale and thin his grey moustache close clipped his eyesight unimpaired <\s>
<s> a slight stoop closened and corrected the expansion given to his face by the heightening of his forehead in the recession of his grey hair <\s>
<s> little change had time wrought in the warmest of the young forsytes as the last of the old forsytes timothy now in his hundred and first year would have phrased it <\s>
<s> the shade from the plane trees fell on his neat homburg hat he had given up top hats it was no use attracting attention to wealth in days like these <\s>
<s> his thoughts travelled sharply to madrid the easter before the war when having to make up his mind about that goya picture he had taken a voyage of discovery to study the painter on his spot <\s>
<s> the fellow had impressed him great range real genius <\s>
<s> highly as the chap ranked he would rank even higher before they had finished with him <\s>
<s> the second goya craze would be greater even than the first oh yes <\s>
<s> and he had bought <\s>
<s> on that visit he had as never before commissioned a copy of a fresco painting called la vendimia wherein was the figure of a girl with an arm akimbo who had reminded him of his daughter <\s>
<s> he had it now in the gallery at mapledurham and rather poor it was you couldn't copy goya <\s>
<s> he would still look at it however if his daughter were not there for the sake of something irresistibly reminiscent in the light erect balance of the figure the width between the arching eyebrows the eager dreaming of the dark eyes <\s>
<s> curious that fleur should have dark eyes when his own were grey no pure forsyte had brown eyes and her mother's blue <\s>
<s> but of course her grandmother lamotte's eyes were dark as treacle <\s>
<s> he began to walk on again toward hyde park corner <\s>
<s> no greater change in all england than in the row <\s>
<s> born almost within hail of it he could remember it from 1860 on <\s>
<s> brought there as a child between the crinolines to stare at tight trousered dandies in whiskers riding with a cavalry seat to watch the doffing of curly brimmed and white top hats the leisurely air of it all and the little bow legged man in a long red waistcoat who used to come among the fashion with dogs on several strings and try to sell one to his mother king charles spaniels italian greyhounds affectionate to her crinoline you never saw them now <\s>
<s> you saw no quality of any sort indeed just working people sitting in dull rows with nothing to stare at but a few young bouncing females in pot hats riding astride or desultory colonials charging up and down on dismal looking hacks with here and there little girls on ponies or old gentlemen jogging their livers or an orderly trying a great galumphing cavalry horse no thoroughbreds no grooms no bowing no scraping no gossip nothing only the trees the same the trees indifferent to the generations and declensions of mankind <\s>
<s> a democratic england dishevelled hurried noisy and seemingly without an apex <\s>
<s> and that something fastidious in the soul of soames turned over within him <\s>
<s> gone forever the close borough of rank and polish <\s>

<s> indeed if he ever thought of such a calamity it was seasoned by the vague feeling that he could make her rich enough to purchase perhaps and extinguish the name of the fellow who married her why not since as it seemed women were equal to men nowadays <\s>
<s> and soames secretly convinced that they were not passed his curved hand over his face vigorously till it reached the comfort of his chin <\s>
<s> thanks to abstemious habits he had not grown fat and gabby his nose was pale and thin his grey moustache close clipped his eyesight unimpaired <\s>
<s> a slight stoop closened and corrected the expansion given to his face by the heightening of his forehead in the recession of his grey hair <\s>
<s> little change had time wrought in the warmest of the young forsytes as the last of the old forsytes timothy now in his hundred and first year would have phrased it <\s>
<s> the shade from the plane trees fell on his neat homburg hat he had given up top hats it was no use attracting attention to wealth in days like these <\s>
<s> his thoughts travelled sharply to madrid the easter before the war when having to make up his mind about that goya picture he had taken a voyage of discovery to study the painter on his spot <\s>
<s> the fellow had impressed him great range real genius <\s>
<s> highly as the chap ranked he would rank even higher before they had finished with him <\s>
<s> the second goya craze would be greater even than the first oh yes <\s>
<s> and he had bought <\s>
<s> on that visit he had as never before commissioned a copy of a fresco painting called la vendimia wherein was the figure of a girl with an arm akimbo who had reminded him of his daughter <\s>
<s> he had it now in the gallery at mapledurham and rather poor it was you couldn't copy goya <\s>
<s> he would still look at it however if his daughter were not there for the sake of something irresistibly reminiscent in the light erect balance of the figure the width between the arching eyebrows the eager dreaming of the dark eyes <\s>
<s> curious that fleur should have dark eyes when his own were grey no pure forsyte had brown eyes and her mother's blue <\s>
<s> but of course her grandmother lamotte's eyes were dark as treacle <\s>
<s> he began to walk on again toward hyde park corner <\s>
<s> no greater change in all england than in the row <\s>
<s> born almost within hail of it he could remember it from 1860 on <\s>
<s> brought there as a child between the crinolines to stare at tight trousered dandies in whiskers riding with a cavalry seat to watch the doffing of curly brimmed and white top hats the leisurely air of it all and the little bow legged man in a long red waistcoat who used to come among the fashion with dogs on several strings and try to sell one to his mother king charles spaniels italian greyhounds affectionate to her crinoline you never saw them now <\s>
<s> you saw no quality of any sort indeed just working people sitting in dull rows with nothing to stare at but a few young bouncing females in pot hats riding astride or desultory colonials charging up and down on dismal looking hacks with here and there little girls on ponies or old gentlemen jogging their livers or an orderly trying a great galumphing cavalry horse no thoroughbreds no grooms no bowing no scraping no gossip nothing only the trees the same the trees indifferent to the generations and declensions of mankind <\s>
<s> a democratic england dishevelled hurried noisy and seemingly without an apex <\s>
<s> and that something fastidious in the soul of soames turned over within him <\s>
<s> gone forever the close borough of rank and polish <\s>
<s> wealth there was oh yes <\s>
<s> wealth he himself was a richer man than his father had ever been but manners flavour quality all gone engulfed in one vast ugly shoulder rubbing petrol smelling cheerio <\s>
<s> little half beaten pockets of gentility and caste lurking here and there dispersed and chetif as annette would say but nothing ever again firm and coherent to look up to <\s>
<s> and into this new hurly burly of bad manners and loose morals his daughter flower of his life was flung <\s>
<s> and when those labour chaps got power if they ever did the worst was yet to come <\s>
<s> he passed out under the archway at last no longer thank goodness disfigured by the gungrey of its search light <\s>
<s> they'd better put a search light on to where they're all going he thought and light up their precious democracy <\s>
<s> and he directed his steps along the club fronts of piccadilly <\s>
<s> george forsyte of course would be sitting in the bay window of the iseeum <\s>
<s> the chap was so big now that he was there nearly all his time like some immovable sardonic humorous eye noting the decline of men and things <\s>
<s> and soames hurried ever constitutionally uneasy beneath his cousin's glance <\s>
<s> george who as he had heard had written a letter signed patriot in the middle of the war complaining of the government's hysteria in docking the oats of race horses <\s>
<s> yes there he was tall ponderous neat clean shaven with his smooth hair hardly thinned smelling no doubt of the best hair wash and a pink paper in his hand <\s>
<s> well he didn't change <\s>
<s> and for perhaps the first time in his life soames felt a kind of sympathy tapping in his waistcoat for that sardonic kinsman <\s>
<s> with his weight his perfectly parted hair and bull like gaze he was a guarantee that the old order would take some shifting yet <\s>
<s> he saw george move the pink paper as if inviting him to ascend the chap must want to ask something about his property <\s>
<s> it was still under soames control for in the adoption of a sleeping partnership at that painful period twenty years back when he had divorced irene soames had found himself almost insensibly retaining control of all purely forsyte affairs <\s>
<s> hesitating for just a moment he nodded and went in <\s>
<s> since the death of his brother in law montague dartie in paris which no one had quite known what to make of except that it was certainly not suicide the iseeum club had seemed more respectable to soames <\s>
<s> george too he knew had sown the last of his wild oats and was committed definitely to the joys of the table eating only of the very best so as to keep his weight down and owning as he said just one or two old screws to give me an interest in life <\s>
<s> he joined his cousin therefore in the bay window without the embarrassing sense of indiscretion he had been used to feel up there <\s>
<s> george put out a well kept hand <\s>
<s> haven't seen you since the war he said <\s>
<s> thanks said soames coldly well enough <\s>
<s> some hidden jest curved for a moment george's fleshy face and gloated from his eye <\s>
<s> that belgian chap profond he said is a member here now <\s>
<s> he's a rum customer <\s>
<s> what did you want to see me about <\s>
<s> old timothy he might go off the hooks at any moment <\s>
<s> i suppose he's made his will <\s>
<s> well you or somebody ought to give him a look up last of the old lot he's a hundred you know <\s>
<s> they say he's like a mummy <\s>
<s> where are you goin to put him <\s>
<s> he ought to have a pyramid by rights <\s>
<s> soames shook his head <\s>
<s> highgate the family vault <\s>
<s> well i suppose the old girls would miss him if he was anywhere else <\s>
<s> they say he still takes an interest in food <\s>
<s> he might last on you know <\s>
<s> don't we get anything for the old forsytes <\s>
<s> ten of them average age eighty eight i worked it out <\s>
<s> that ought to be equal to triplets <\s>
<s> said soames i must be getting on <\s>
<s> you unsociable devil george's eyes seemed to answer <\s>
<s> yes that's all look him up in his mausoleum the old chap might want to prophesy <\s>
<s> the grin died on the rich curves of his face and he added haven't you attorneys invented a way yet of dodging this damned income tax <\s>
<s> it hits the fixed inherited income like the very deuce <\s>
<s> i used to have two thousand five hundred a year now i've got a beggarly fifteen hundred and the price of living doubled <\s>
<s> his wife was always out when she was in town and his daughter would flibberty gibbet all over the place like most young women since the war <\s>
<s> still he must be thankful that she had been too young to do anything in that war itself <\s>
<s> not of course that he had not supported the war from its inception with all his soul but between that and supporting it with the bodies of his wife and daughter there had been a gap fixed by something old fashioned within him which abhorred emotional extravagance <\s>
<s> he had for instance strongly objected to annette so attractive and in 1914 only thirty four going to her native france her chere patrie as under the stimulus of war she had begun to call it to nurse her braves poilus forsooth <\s>
<s> ruining her health and her looks <\s>
<s> as if she were really a nurse <\s>
<s> he had put a stopper on it <\s>
<s> let her do needlework for them at home or knit <\s>
<s> she had not gone therefore and had never been quite the same woman since <\s>
<s> a bad tendency of hers to mock at him not openly but in continual little ways had grown <\s>
<s> as for fleur the war had resolved the vexed problem whether or not she should go to school <\s>
<s> she was better away from her mother in her war mood from the chance of air raids and the impetus to do extravagant things so he had placed her in a seminary as far west as had seemed to him compatible with excellence and had missed her horribly <\s>
<s> he had never regretted the somewhat outlandish name by which at her birth he had decided so suddenly to call her marked concession though it had been to the french <\s>
<s> a pretty name a pretty child <\s>
<s> but restless too restless and wilful <\s>
<s> knowing her power too over her father <\s>
<s> soames often reflected on the mistake it was to dote on his daughter <\s>
<s> to get old and dote <\s>
<s> he was getting on but he didn't feel it for fortunately perhaps considering annette's youth and good looks his second marriage had turned out a cool affair <\s>
<s> he had known but one real passion in his life for that first wife of his irene <\s>
<s> yes and that fellow his cousin jolyon who had gone off with her was looking very shaky they said <\s>

<s> it hits the fixed inherited income like the very deuce <\s>
<s> i used to have two thousand five hundred a year now i've got a beggarly fifteen hundred and the price of living doubled <\s>
<s> his wife was always out when she was in town and his daughter would flibberty gibbet all over the place like most young women since the war <\s>
<s> still he must be thankful that she had been too young to do anything in that war itself <\s>
<s> not of course that he had not supported the war from its inception with all his soul but between that and supporting it with the bodies of his wife and daughter there had been a gap fixed by something old fashioned within him which abhorred emotional extravagance <\s>
<s> he had for instance strongly objected to annette so attractive and in 1914 only thirty four going to her native france her chere patrie as under the stimulus of war she had begun to call it to nurse her braves poilus forsooth <\s>
<s> ruining her health and her looks <\s>
<s> as if she were really a nurse <\s>
<s> he had put a stopper on it <\s>
<s> let her do needlework for them at home or knit <\s>
<s> she had not gone therefore and had never been quite the same woman since <\s>
<s> a bad tendency of hers to mock at him not openly but in continual little ways had grown <\s>
<s> as for fleur the war had resolved the vexed problem whether or not she should go to school <\s>
<s> she was better away from her mother in her war mood from the chance of air raids and the impetus to do extravagant things so he had placed her in a seminary as far west as had seemed to him compatible with excellence and had missed her horribly <\s>
<s> he had never regretted the somewhat outlandish name by which at her birth he had decided so suddenly to call her marked concession though it had been to the french <\s>
<s> a pretty name a pretty child <\s>
<s> but restless too restless and wilful <\s>
<s> knowing her power too over her father <\s>
<s> soames often reflected on the mistake it was to dote on his daughter <\s>
<s> to get old and dote <\s>
<s> he was getting on but he didn't feel it for fortunately perhaps considering annette's youth and good looks his second marriage had turned out a cool affair <\s>
<s> he had known but one real passion in his life for that first wife of his irene <\s>
<s> yes and that fellow his cousin jolyon who had gone off with her was looking very shaky they said <\s>
<s> no wonder at seventy two after twenty years of a third marriage <\s>
<s> soames paused a moment in his march to lean over the railings of the row <\s>
<s> a suitable spot for reminiscence half way between that house in park lane which had seen his birth and his parents deaths and the little house in montpellier square where thirty five years ago he had enjoyed his first edition of matrimony <\s>
<s> now after twenty years of his second edition that old tragedy seemed to him like a previous existence which had ended when fleur was born in place of the son he had hoped for <\s>
<s> for many years he had ceased regretting even vaguely the son who had not been born fleur filled the bill in his heart <\s>
<s> after all she bore his name and he was not looking forward at all to the time when she would change it <\s>
<s> indeed if he ever thought of such a calamity it was seasoned by the vague feeling that he could make her rich enough to purchase perhaps and extinguish the name of the fellow who married her why not since as it seemed women were equal to men nowadays <\s>
<s> and soames secretly convinced that they were not passed his curved hand over his face vigorously till it reached the comfort of his chin <\s>
<s> thanks to abstemious habits he had not grown fat and gabby his nose was pale and thin his grey moustache close clipped his eyesight unimpaired <\s>
<s> a slight stoop closened and corrected the expansion given to his face by the heightening of his forehead in the recession of his grey hair <\s>
<s> little change had time wrought in the warmest of the young forsytes as the last of the old forsytes timothy now in his hundred and first year would have phrased it <\s>
<s> the shade from the plane trees fell on his neat homburg hat he had given up top hats it was no use attracting attention to wealth in days like these <\s>
<s> his thoughts travelled sharply to madrid the easter before the war when having to make up his mind about that goya picture he had taken a voyage of discovery to study the painter on his spot <\s>
<s> the fellow had impressed him great range real genius <\s>
<s> highly as the chap ranked he would rank even higher before they had finished with him <\s>
<s> the second goya craze would be greater even than the first oh yes <\s>
<s> and he had bought <\s>
<s> on that visit he had as never before commissioned a copy of a fresco painting called la vendimia wherein was the figure of a girl with an arm akimbo who had reminded him of his daughter <\s>
<s> he had it now in the gallery at mapledurham and rather poor it was you couldn't copy goya <\s>
<s> he would still look at it however if his daughter were not there for the sake of something irresistibly reminiscent in the light erect balance of the figure the width between the arching eyebrows the eager dreaming of the dark eyes <\s>
<s> curious that fleur should have dark eyes when his own were grey no pure forsyte had brown eyes and her mother's blue <\s>
<s> but of course her grandmother lamotte's eyes were dark as treacle <\s>
<s> he began to walk on again toward hyde park corner <\s>
<s> no greater change in all england than in the row <\s>
<s> born almost within hail of it he could remember it from 1860 on <\s>
<s> brought there as a child between the crinolines to stare at tight trousered dandies in whiskers riding with a cavalry seat to watch the doffing of curly brimmed and white top hats the leisurely air of it all and the little bow legged man in a long red waistcoat who used to come among the fashion with dogs on several strings and try to sell one to his mother king charles spaniels italian greyhounds affectionate to her crinoline you never saw them now <\s>
<s> you saw no quality of any sort indeed just working people sitting in dull rows with nothing to stare at but a few young bouncing females in pot hats riding astride or desultory colonials charging up and down on dismal looking hacks with here and there little girls on ponies or old gentlemen jogging their livers or an orderly trying a great galumphing cavalry horse no thoroughbreds no grooms no bowing no scraping no gossip nothing only the trees the same the trees indifferent to the generations and declensions of mankind <\s>
<s> a democratic england dishevelled hurried noisy and seemingly without an apex <\s>
<s> and that something fastidious in the soul of soames turned over within him <\s>
<s> gone forever the close borough of rank and polish <\s>
<s> wealth there was oh yes <\s>
<s> wealth he himself was a richer man than his father had ever been but manners flavour quality all gone engulfed in one vast ugly shoulder rubbing petrol smelling cheerio <\s>
<s> little half beaten pockets of gentility and caste lurking here and there dispersed and chetif as annette would say but nothing ever again firm and coherent to look up to <\s>

<s> and when those labour chaps got power if they ever did the worst was yet to come <\s>

<s> you saw no quality of any sort indeed just working people sitting in dull rows with nothing to stare at but a few young bouncing females in pot hats riding astride or desultory colonials charging up and down on dismal looking hacks with here and there little girls on ponies or old gentlemen jogging their livers or an orderly trying a great galumphing cavalry horse no thoroughbreds no grooms no bowing no scraping no gossip nothing only the trees the same the trees indifferent to the generations and declensions of mankind <\s>
<s> a democratic england dishevelled hurried noisy and seemingly without an apex <\s>
<s> and that something fastidious in the soul of soames turned over within him <\s>
<s> gone forever the close borough of rank and polish <\s>
<s> wealth there was oh yes <\s>
<s> wealth he himself was a richer man than his father had ever been but manners flavour quality all gone engulfed in one vast ugly shoulder rubbing petrol smelling cheerio <\s>
<s> little half beaten pockets of gentility and caste lurking here and there dispersed and chetif as annette would say but nothing ever again firm and coherent to look up to <\s>
<s> and into this new hurly burly of bad manners and loose morals his daughter flower of his life was flung <\s>
<s> and when those labour chaps got power if they ever did the worst was yet to come <\s>
<s> he passed out under the archway at last no longer thank goodness disfigured by the gungrey of its search light <\s>
<s> they'd better put a search light on to where they're all going he thought and light up their precious democracy <\s>
<s> and he directed his steps along the club fronts of piccadilly <\s>
<s> george forsyte of course would be sitting in the bay window of the iseeum <\s>
<s> the chap was so big now that he was there nearly all his time like some immovable sardonic humorous eye noting the decline of men and things <\s>
<s> and soames hurried ever constitutionally uneasy beneath his cousin's glance <\s>
<s> george who as he had heard had written a letter signed patriot in the middle of the war complaining of the government's hysteria in docking the oats of race horses <\s>
<s> yes there he was tall ponderous neat clean shaven with his smooth hair hardly thinned smelling no doubt of the best hair wash and a pink paper in his hand <\s>
<s> well he didn't change <\s>
<s> and for perhaps the first time in his life soames felt a kind of sympathy tapping in his waistcoat for that sardonic kinsman <\s>
<s> with his weight his perfectly parted hair and bull like gaze he was a guarantee that the old order would take some shifting yet <\s>
<s> he saw george move the pink paper as if inviting him to ascend the chap must want to ask something about his property <\s>
<s> it was still under soames control for in the adoption of a sleeping partnership at that painful period twenty years back when he had divorced irene soames had found himself almost insensibly retaining control of all purely forsyte affairs <\s>
<s> hesitating for just a moment he nodded and went in <\s>
<s> since the death of his brother in law montague dartie in paris which no one had quite known what to make of except that it was certainly not suicide the iseeum club had seemed more respectable to soames <\s>
<s> george too he knew had sown the last of his wild oats and was committed definitely to the joys of the table eating only of the very best so as to keep his weight down and owning as he said just one or two old screws to give me an interest in life <\s>
<s> he joined his cousin therefore in the bay window without the embarrassing sense of indiscretion he had been used to feel up there <\s>
<s> george put out a well kept hand <\s>
<s> haven't seen you since the war he said <\s>
<s> thanks said soames coldly well enough <\s>
<s> some hidden jest curved for a moment george's fleshy face and gloated from his eye <\s>
<s> that belgian chap profond he said is a member here now <\s>
<s> he's a rum customer <\s>
<s> what did you want to see me about <\s>
<s> old timothy he might go off the hooks at any moment <\s>
<s> i suppose he's made his will <\s>
<s> well you or somebody ought to give him a look up last of the old lot he's a hundred you know <\s>
<s> they say he's like a mummy <\s>
<s> where are you goin to put him <\s>
<s> he ought to have a pyramid by rights <\s>
<s> soames shook his head <\s>
<s> highgate the family vault <\s>
<s> well i suppose the old girls would miss him if he was anywhere else <\s>
<s> they say he still takes an interest in food <\s>
<s> he might last on you know <\s>
<s> don't we get anything for the old forsytes <\s>
<s> ten of them average age eighty eight i worked it out <\s>
<s> that ought to be equal to triplets <\s>
<s> said soames i must be getting on <\s>
<s> you unsociable devil george's eyes seemed to answer <\s>
<s> yes that's all look him up in his mausoleum the old chap might want to prophesy <\s>
<s> the grin died on the rich curves of his face and he added haven't you attorneys invented a way yet of dodging this damned income tax <\s>
<s> it hits the fixed inherited income like the very deuce <\s>
<s> i used to have two thousand five hundred a year now i've got a beggarly fifteen hundred and the price of living doubled <\s>
<s> his wife was always out when she was in town and his daughter would flibberty gibbet all over the place like most young women since the war <\s>
<s> still he must be thankful that she had been too young to do anything in that war itself <\s>
<s> not of course that he had not supported the war from its inception with all his soul but between that and supporting it with the bodies of his wife and daughter there had been a gap fixed by something old fashioned within him which abhorred emotional extravagance <\s>
<s> he had for instance strongly objected to annette so attractive and in 1914 only thirty four going to her native france her chere patrie as under the stimulus of war she had begun to call it to nurse her braves poilus forsooth <\s>
<s> ruining her health and her looks <\s>
<s> as if she were really a nurse <\s>
<s> he had put a stopper on it <\s>
<s> let her do needlework for them at home or knit <\s>
<s> she had not gone therefore and had never been quite the same woman since <\s>
<s> a bad tendency of hers to mock at him not openly but in continual little ways had grown <\s>
<s> as for fleur the war had resolved the vexed problem whether or not she should go to school <\s>
<s> she was better away from her mother in her war mood from the chance of air raids and the impetus to do extravagant things so he had placed her in a seminary as far west as had seemed to him compatible with excellence and had missed her horribly <\s>
<s> he had never regretted the somewhat outlandish name by which at her birth he had decided so suddenly to call her marked concession though it had been to the french <\s>
<s> a pretty name a pretty child <\s>
<s> but restless too restless and wilful <\s>
<s> knowing her power too over her father <\s>
<s> soames often reflected on the mistake it was to dote on his daughter <\s>
<s> to get old and dote <\s>
<s> he was getting on but he didn't feel it for fortunately perhaps considering annette's youth and good looks his second marriage had turned out a cool affair <\s>
<s> he had known but one real passion in his life for that first wife of his irene <\s>
<s> yes and that fellow his cousin jolyon who had gone off with her was looking very shaky they said <\s>
<s> no wonder at seventy two after twenty years of a third marriage <\s>
<s> soames paused a moment in his march to lean over the railings of the row <\s>
<s> a suitable spot for reminiscence half way between that house in park lane which had seen his birth and his parents deaths and the little house in montpellier square where thirty five years ago he had enjoyed his first edition of matrimony <\s>
<s> now after twenty years of his second edition that old tragedy seemed to him like a previous existence which had ended when fleur was born in place of the son he had hoped for <\s>
<s> for many years he had ceased regretting even vaguely the son who had not been born fleur filled the bill in his heart <\s>
<s> after all she bore his name and he was not looking forward at all to the time when she would change it <\s>
<s> indeed if he ever thought of such a calamity it was seasoned by the vague feeling that he could make her rich enough to purchase perhaps and extinguish the name of the fellow who married her why not since as it seemed women were equal to men nowadays <\s>
<s> and soames secretly convinced that they were not passed his curved hand over his face vigorously till it reached the comfort of his chin <\s>
<s> thanks to abstemious habits he had not grown fat and gabby his nose was pale and thin his grey moustache close clipped his eyesight unimpaired <\s>
<s> a slight stoop closened and corrected the expansion given to his face by the heightening of his forehead in the recession of his grey hair <\s>
<s> little change had time wrought in the warmest of the young forsytes as the last of the old forsytes timothy now in his hundred and first year would have phrased it <\s>
<s> the shade from the plane trees fell on his neat homburg hat he had given up top hats it was no use attracting attention to wealth in days like these <\s>
<s> his thoughts travelled sharply to madrid the easter before the war when having to make up his mind about that goya picture he had taken a voyage of discovery to study the painter on his spot <\s>
<s> the fellow had impressed him great range real genius <\s>
<s> highly as the chap ranked he would rank even higher before they had finished with him <\s>
<s> the second goya craze would be greater even than the first oh yes <\s>
<s> and he had bought <\s>
<s> on that visit he had as never before commissioned a copy of a fresco painting called la vendimia wherein was the figure of a girl with an arm akimbo who had reminded him of his daughter <\s>
<s> he had it now in the gallery at mapledurham and rather poor it was you couldn't copy goya <\s>
<s> he would still look at it however if his daughter were not there for the sake of something irresistibly reminiscent in the light erect balance of the figure the width between the arching eyebrows the eager dreaming of the dark eyes <\s>
<s> curious that fleur should have dark eyes when his own were grey no pure forsyte had brown eyes and her mother's blue <\s>
<s> but of course her grandmother lamotte's eyes were dark as treacle <\s>

<s> she was better away from her mother in her war mood from the chance of air raids and the impetus to do extravagant things so he had placed her in a seminary as far west as had seemed to him compatible with excellence and had missed her horribly <\s>
<s> he had never regretted the somewhat outlandish name by which at her birth he had decided so suddenly to call her marked concession though it had been to the french <\s>
<s> a pretty name a pretty child <\s>
<s> but restless too restless and wilful <\s>
<s> knowing her power too over her father <\s>
<s> soames often reflected on the mistake it was to dote on his daughter <\s>
<s> to get old and dote <\s>
<s> he was getting on but he didn't feel it for fortunately perhaps considering annette's youth and good looks his second marriage had turned out a cool affair <\s>
<s> he had known but one real passion in his life for that first wife of his irene <\s>
<s> yes and that fellow his cousin jolyon who had gone off with her was looking very shaky they said <\s>
<s> no wonder at seventy two after twenty years of a third marriage <\s>
<s> soames paused a moment in his march to lean over the railings of the row <\s>
<s> a suitable spot for reminiscence half way between that house in park lane which had seen his birth and his parents deaths and the little house in montpellier square where thirty five years ago he had enjoyed his first edition of matrimony <\s>
<s> now after twenty years of his second edition that old tragedy seemed to him like a previous existence which had ended when fleur was born in place of the son he had hoped for <\s>
<s> for many years he had ceased regretting even vaguely the son who had not been born fleur filled the bill in his heart <\s>
<s> after all she bore his name and he was not looking forward at all to the time when she would change it <\s>
<s> indeed if he ever thought of such a calamity it was seasoned by the vague feeling that he could make her rich enough to purchase perhaps and extinguish the name of the fellow who married her why not since as it seemed women were equal to men nowadays <\s>
<s> and soames secretly convinced that they were not passed his curved hand over his face vigorously till it reached the comfort of his chin <\s>
<s> thanks to abstemious habits he had not grown fat and gabby his nose was pale and thin his grey moustache close clipped his eyesight unimpaired <\s>
<s> a slight stoop closened and corrected the expansion given to his face by the heightening of his forehead in the recession of his grey hair <\s>
<s> little change had time wrought in the warmest of the young forsytes as the last of the old forsytes timothy now in his hundred and first year would have phrased it <\s>
<s> the shade from the plane trees fell on his neat homburg hat he had given up top hats it was no use attracting attention to wealth in days like these <\s>
<s> his thoughts travelled sharply to madrid the easter before the war when having to make up his mind about that goya picture he had taken a voyage of discovery to study the painter on his spot <\s>
<s> the fellow had impressed him great range real genius <\s>
<s> highly as the chap ranked he would rank even higher before they had finished with him <\s>
<s> the second goya craze would be greater even than the first oh yes <\s>
<s> and he had bought <\s>
<s> on that visit he had as never before commissioned a copy of a fresco painting called la vendimia wherein was the figure of a girl with an arm akimbo who had reminded him of his daughter <\s>
<s> he had it now in the gallery at mapledurham and rather poor it was you couldn't copy goya <\s>
<s> he would still look at it however if his daughter were not there for the sake of something irresistibly reminiscent in the light erect balance of the figure the width between the arching eyebrows the eager dreaming of the dark eyes <\s>
<s> curious that fleur should have dark eyes when his own were grey no pure forsyte had brown eyes and her mother's blue <\s>
<s> but of course her grandmother lamotte's eyes were dark as treacle <\s>
<s> he began to walk on again toward hyde park corner <\s>
<s> no greater change in all england than in the row <\s>
<s> born almost within hail of it he could remember it from 1860 on <\s>
<s> brought there as a child between the crinolines to stare at tight trousered dandies in whiskers riding with a cavalry seat to watch the doffing of curly brimmed and white top hats the leisurely air of it all and the little bow legged man in a long red waistcoat who used to come among the fashion with dogs on several strings and try to sell one to his mother king charles spaniels italian greyhounds affectionate to her crinoline you never saw them now <\s>
<s> you saw no quality of any sort indeed just working people sitting in dull rows with nothing to stare at but a few young bouncing females in pot hats riding astride or desultory colonials charging up and down on dismal looking hacks with here and there little girls on ponies or old gentlemen jogging their livers or an orderly trying a great galumphing cavalry horse no thoroughbreds no grooms no bowing no scraping no gossip nothing only the trees the same the trees indifferent to the generations and declensions of mankind <\s>
<s> a democratic england dishevelled hurried noisy and seemingly without an apex <\s>
<s> and that something fastidious in the soul of soames turned over within him <\s>
<s> gone forever the close borough of rank and polish <\s>
<s> wealth there was oh yes <\s>
<s> wealth he himself was a richer man than his father had ever been but manners flavour quality all gone engulfed in one vast ugly shoulder rubbing petrol smelling cheerio <\s>
<s> little half beaten pockets of gentility and caste lurking here and there dispersed and chetif as annette would say but nothing ever again firm and coherent to look up to <\s>
<s> and into this new hurly burly of bad manners and loose morals his daughter flower of his life was flung <\s>
<s> and when those labour chaps got power if they ever did the worst was yet to come <\s>
<s> he passed out under the archway at last no longer thank goodness disfigured by the gungrey of its search light <\s>
<s> they'd better put a search light on to where they're all going he thought and light up their precious democracy <\s>
<s> and he directed his steps along the club fronts of piccadilly <\s>
<s> george forsyte of course would be sitting in the bay window of the iseeum <\s>
<s> the chap was so big now that he was there nearly all his time like some immovable sardonic humorous eye noting the decline of men and things <\s>
<s> and soames hurried ever constitutionally uneasy beneath his cousin's glance <\s>
<s> george who as he had heard had written a letter signed patriot in the middle of the war complaining of the government's hysteria in docking the oats of race horses <\s>
<s> yes there he was tall ponderous neat clean shaven with his smooth hair hardly thinned smelling no doubt of the best hair wash and a pink paper in his hand <\s>
<s> well he didn't change <\s>
<s> and for perhaps the first time in his life soames felt a kind of sympathy tapping in his waistcoat for that sardonic kinsman <\s>
<s> with his weight his perfectly parted hair and bull like gaze he was a guarantee that the old order would take some shifting yet <\s>
<s> he saw george move the pink paper as if inviting him to ascend the chap must want to ask something about his property <\s>
<s> it was still under soames control for in the adoption of a sleeping partnership at that painful period twenty years back when he had divorced irene soames had found himself almost insensibly retaining control of all purely forsyte affairs <\s>
<s> hesitating for just a moment he nodded and went in <\s>
<s> since the death of his brother in law montague dartie in paris which no one had quite known what to make of except that it was certainly not suicide the iseeum club had seemed more respectable to soames <\s>
<s> george too he knew had sown the last of his wild oats and was committed definitely to the joys of the table eating only of the very best so as to keep his weight down and owning as he said just one or two old screws to give me an interest in life <\s>

<s> he saw george move the pink paper as if inviting him to ascend the chap must want to ask something about his property <\s>

<s> the grin died on the rich curves of his face and he added haven't you attorneys invented a way yet of dodging this damned income tax <\s>
<s> it hits the fixed inherited income like the very deuce <\s>
<s> i used to have two thousand five hundred a year now i've got a beggarly fifteen hundred and the price of living doubled <\s>
<s> his wife was always out when she was in town and his daughter would flibberty gibbet all over the place like most young women since the war <\s>
<s> still he must be thankful that she had been too young to do anything in that war itself <\s>
<s> not of course that he had not supported the war from its inception with all his soul but between that and supporting it with the bodies of his wife and daughter there had been a gap fixed by something old fashioned within him which abhorred emotional extravagance <\s>
<s> he had for instance strongly objected to annette so attractive and in 1914 only thirty four going to her native france her chere patrie as under the stimulus of war she had begun to call it to nurse her braves poilus forsooth <\s>
<s> ruining her health and her looks <\s>
<s> as if she were really a nurse <\s>
<s> he had put a stopper on it <\s>
<s> let her do needlework for them at home or knit <\s>
<s> she had not gone therefore and had never been quite the same woman since <\s>
<s> a bad tendency of hers to mock at him not openly but in continual little ways had grown <\s>
<s> as for fleur the war had resolved the vexed problem whether or not she should go to school <\s>
<s> she was better away from her mother in her war mood from the chance of air raids and the impetus to do extravagant things so he had placed her in a seminary as far west as had seemed to him compatible with excellence and had missed her horribly <\s>
<s> he had never regretted the somewhat outlandish name by which at her birth he had decided so suddenly to call her marked concession though it had been to the french <\s>
<s> a pretty name a pretty child <\s>
<s> but restless too restless and wilful <\s>
<s> knowing her power too over her father <\s>
<s> soames often reflected on the mistake it was to dote on his daughter <\s>
<s> to get old and dote <\s>
<s> he was getting on but he didn't feel it for fortunately perhaps considering annette's youth and good looks his second marriage had turned out a cool affair <\s>
<s> he had known but one real passion in his life for that first wife of his irene <\s>
<s> yes and that fellow his cousin jolyon who had gone off with her was looking very shaky they said <\s>
<s> no wonder at seventy two after twenty years of a third marriage <\s>
<s> soames paused a moment in his march to lean over the railings of the row <\s>
<s> a suitable spot for reminiscence half way between that house in park lane which had seen his birth and his parents deaths and the little house in montpellier square where thirty five years ago he had enjoyed his first edition of matrimony <\s>
<s> now after twenty years of his second edition that old tragedy seemed to him like a previous existence which had ended when fleur was born in place of the son he had hoped for <\s>
<s> for many years he had ceased regretting even vaguely the son who had not been born fleur filled the bill in his heart <\s>
<s> after all she bore his name and he was not looking forward at all to the time when she would change it <\s>
<s> indeed if he ever thought of such a calamity it was seasoned by the vague feeling that he could make her rich enough to purchase perhaps and extinguish the name of the fellow who married her why not since as it seemed women were equal to men nowadays <\s>
<s> and soames secretly convinced that they were not passed his curved hand over his face vigorously till it reached the comfort of his chin <\s>
<s> thanks to abstemious habits he had not grown fat and gabby his nose was pale and thin his grey moustache close clipped his eyesight unimpaired <\s>
<s> a slight stoop closened and corrected the expansion given to his face by the heightening of his forehead in the recession of his grey hair <\s>
<s> little change had time wrought in the warmest of the young forsytes as the last of the old forsytes timothy now in his hundred and first year would have phrased it <\s>
<s> the shade from the plane trees fell on his neat homburg hat he had given up top hats it was no use attracting attention to wealth in days like these <\s>

<s> the fellow had impressed him great range real genius <\s>

<s> he had it now in the gallery at mapledurham and rather poor it was you couldn't copy goya <\s>
<s> he would still look at it however if his daughter were not there for the sake of something irresistibly reminiscent in the light erect balance of the figure the width between the arching eyebrows the eager dreaming of the dark eyes <\s>
<s> curious that fleur should have dark eyes when his own were grey no pure forsyte had brown eyes and her mother's blue <\s>
<s> but of course her grandmother lamotte's eyes were dark as treacle <\s>
<s> he began to walk on again toward hyde park corner <\s>
<s> no greater change in all england than in the row <\s>
<s> born almost within hail of it he could remember it from 1860 on <\s>
<s> brought there as a child between the crinolines to stare at tight trousered dandies in whiskers riding with a cavalry seat to watch the doffing of curly brimmed and white top hats the leisurely air of it all and the little bow legged man in a long red waistcoat who used to come among the fashion with dogs on several strings and try to sell one to his mother king charles spaniels italian greyhounds affectionate to her crinoline you never saw them now <\s>
<s> you saw no quality of any sort indeed just working people sitting in dull rows with nothing to stare at but a few young bouncing females in pot hats riding astride or desultory colonials charging up and down on dismal looking hacks with here and there little girls on ponies or old gentlemen jogging their livers or an orderly trying a great galumphing cavalry horse no thoroughbreds no grooms no bowing no scraping no gossip nothing only the trees the same the trees indifferent to the generations and declensions of mankind <\s>

<s> his thoughts travelled sharply to madrid the easter before the war when having to make up his mind about that goya picture he had taken a voyage of discovery to study the painter on his spot <\s>
<s> the fellow had impressed him great range real genius <\s>
<s> highly as the chap ranked he would rank even higher before they had finished with him <\s>
<s> the second goya craze would be greater even than the first oh yes <\s>
<s> and he had bought <\s>
<s> on that visit he had as never before commissioned a copy of a fresco painting called la vendimia wherein was the figure of a girl with an arm akimbo who had reminded him of his daughter <\s>
<s> he had it now in the gallery at mapledurham and rather poor it was you couldn't copy goya <\s>
<s> he would still look at it however if his daughter were not there for the sake of something irresistibly reminiscent in the light erect balance of the figure the width between the arching eyebrows the eager dreaming of the dark eyes <\s>
<s> curious that fleur should have dark eyes when his own were grey no pure forsyte had brown eyes and her mother's blue <\s>
<s> but of course her grandmother lamotte's eyes were dark as treacle <\s>
<s> he began to walk on again toward hyde park corner <\s>
<s> no greater change in all england than in the row <\s>
<s> born almost within hail of it he could remember it from 1860 on <\s>
<s> brought there as a child between the crinolines to stare at tight trousered dandies in whiskers riding with a cavalry seat to watch the doffing of curly brimmed and white top hats the leisurely air of it all and the little bow legged man in a long red waistcoat who used to come among the fashion with dogs on several strings and try to sell one to his mother king charles spaniels italian greyhounds affectionate to her crinoline you never saw them now <\s>
<s> you saw no quality of any sort indeed just working people sitting in dull rows with nothing to stare at but a few young bouncing females in pot hats riding astride or desultory colonials charging up and down on dismal looking hacks with here and there little girls on ponies or old gentlemen jogging their livers or an orderly trying a great galumphing cavalry horse no thoroughbreds no grooms no bowing no scraping no gossip nothing only the trees the same the trees indifferent to the generations and declensions of mankind <\s>
<s> a democratic england dishevelled hurried noisy and seemingly without an apex <\s>
<s> and that something fastidious in the soul of soames turned over within him <\s>
<s> gone forever the close borough of rank and polish <\s>
<s> wealth there was oh yes <\s>
<s> wealth he himself was a richer man than his father had ever been but manners flavour quality all gone engulfed in one vast ugly shoulder rubbing petrol smelling cheerio <\s>
<s> little half beaten pockets of gentility and caste lurking here and there dispersed and chetif as annette would say but nothing ever again firm and coherent to look up to <\s>
<s> and into this new hurly burly of bad manners and loose morals his daughter flower of his life was flung <\s>
<s> and when those labour chaps got power if they ever did the worst was yet to come <\s>
<s> he passed out under the archway at last no longer thank goodness disfigured by the gungrey of its search light <\s>
<s> they'd better put a search light on to where they're all going he thought and light up their precious democracy <\s>
<s> and he directed his steps along the club fronts of piccadilly <\s>
<s> george forsyte of course would be sitting in the bay window of the iseeum <\s>
<s> the chap was so big now that he was there nearly all his time like some immovable sardonic humorous eye noting the decline of men and things <\s>
<s> and soames hurried ever constitutionally uneasy beneath his cousin's glance <\s>
<s> george who as he had heard had written a letter signed patriot in the middle of the war complaining of the government's hysteria in docking the oats of race horses <\s>
<s> yes there he was tall ponderous neat clean shaven with his smooth hair hardly thinned smelling no doubt of the best hair wash and a pink paper in his hand <\s>
<s> well he didn't change <\s>
<s> and for perhaps the first time in his life soames felt a kind of sympathy tapping in his waistcoat for that sardonic kinsman <\s>
<s> with his weight his perfectly parted hair and bull like gaze he was a guarantee that the old order would take some shifting yet <\s>
<s> he saw george move the pink paper as if inviting him to ascend the chap must want to ask something about his property <\s>
<s> it was still under soames control for in the adoption of a sleeping partnership at that painful period twenty years back when he had divorced irene soames had found himself almost insensibly retaining control of all purely forsyte affairs <\s>
<s> hesitating for just a moment he nodded and went in <\s>
<s> since the death of his brother in law montague dartie in paris which no one had quite known what to make of except that it was certainly not suicide the iseeum club had seemed more respectable to soames <\s>
<s> george too he knew had sown the last of his wild oats and was committed definitely to the joys of the table eating only of the very best so as to keep his weight down and owning as he said just one or two old screws to give me an interest in life <\s>
<s> he joined his cousin therefore in the bay window without the embarrassing sense of indiscretion he had been used to feel up there <\s>
<s> george put out a well kept hand <\s>
<s> haven't seen you since the war he said <\s>
<s> thanks said soames coldly well enough <\s>
<s> some hidden jest curved for a moment george's fleshy face and gloated from his eye <\s>
<s> that belgian chap profond he said is a member here now <\s>
<s> he's a rum customer <\s>
<s> what did you want to see me about <\s>
<s> old timothy he might go off the hooks at any moment <\s>
<s> i suppose he's made his will <\s>
<s> well you or somebody ought to give him a look up last of the old lot he's a hundred you know <\s>
<s> they say he's like a mummy <\s>
<s> where are you goin to put him <\s>
<s> he ought to have a pyramid by rights <\s>
<s> soames shook his head <\s>
<s> highgate the family vault <\s>
<s> well i suppose the old girls would miss him if he was anywhere else <\s>
<s> they say he still takes an interest in food <\s>
<s> he might last on you know <\s>
<s> don't we get anything for the old forsytes <\s>
<s> ten of them average age eighty eight i worked it out <\s>
<s> that ought to be equal to triplets <\s>
<s> said soames i must be getting on <\s>
<s> you unsociable devil george's eyes seemed to answer <\s>
<s> yes that's all look him up in his mausoleum the old chap might want to prophesy <\s>
<s> the grin died on the rich curves of his face and he added haven't you attorneys invented a way yet of dodging this damned income tax <\s>
<s> it hits the fixed inherited income like the very deuce <\s>
<s> i used to have two thousand five hundred a year now i've got a beggarly fifteen hundred and the price of living doubled <\s>
<s> his wife was always out when she was in town and his daughter would flibberty gibbet all over the place like most young women since the war <\s>
<s> still he must be thankful that she had been too young to do anything in that war itself <\s>
<s> not of course that he had not supported the war from its inception with all his soul but between that and supporting it with the bodies of his wife and daughter there had been a gap fixed by something old fashioned within him which abhorred emotional extravagance <\s>
<s> he had for instance strongly objected to annette so attractive and in 1914 only thirty four going to her native france her chere patrie as under the stimulus of war she had begun to call it to nurse her braves poilus forsooth <\s>
<s> ruining her health and her looks <\s>
<s> as if she were really a nurse <\s>
<s> he had put a stopper on it <\s>
<s> let her do needlework for them at home or knit <\s>
<s> she had not gone therefore and had never been quite the same woman since <\s>
<s> a bad tendency of hers to mock at him not openly but in continual little ways had grown <\s>
<s> as for fleur the war had resolved the vexed problem whether or not she should go to school <\s>
<s> she was better away from her mother in her war mood from the chance of air raids and the impetus to do extravagant things so he had placed her in a seminary as far west as had seemed to him compatible with excellence and had missed her horribly <\s>
<s> he had never regretted the somewhat outlandish name by which at her birth he had decided so suddenly to call her marked concession though it had been to the french <\s>
<s> a pretty name a pretty child <\s>
<s> but restless too restless and wilful <\s>
<s> knowing her power too over her father <\s>
<s> soames often reflected on the mistake it was to dote on his daughter <\s>
<s> to get old and dote <\s>
<s> he was getting on but he didn't feel it for fortunately perhaps considering annette's youth and good looks his second marriage had turned out a cool affair <\s>
<s> he had known but one real passion in his life for that first wife of his irene <\s>
<s> yes and that fellow his cousin jolyon who had gone off with her was looking very shaky they said <\s>
<s> no wonder at seventy two after twenty years of a third marriage <\s>
<s> soames paused a moment in his march to lean over the railings of the row <\s>
<s> a suitable spot for reminiscence half way between that house in park lane which had seen his birth and his parents deaths and the little house in montpellier square where thirty five years ago he had enjoyed his first edition of matrimony <\s>
<s> now after twenty years of his second edition that old tragedy seemed to him like a previous existence which had ended when fleur was born in place of the son he had hoped for <\s>
<s> for many years he had ceased regretting even vaguely the son who had not been born fleur filled the bill in his heart <\s>
<s> after all she bore his name and he was not looking forward at all to the time when she would change it <\s>
<s> indeed if he ever thought of such a calamity it was seasoned by the vague feeling that he could make her rich enough to purchase perhaps and extinguish the name of the fellow who married her why not since as it seemed women were equal to men nowadays <\s>
<s> and soames secretly convinced that they were not passed his curved hand over his face vigorously till it reached the comfort of his chin <\s>

<s> it hits the fixed inherited income like the very deuce <\s>
<s> i used to have two thousand five hundred a year now i've got a beggarly fifteen hundred and the price of living doubled <\s>
<s> his wife was always out when she was in town and his daughter would flibberty gibbet all over the place like most young women since the war <\s>
<s> still he must be thankful that she had been too young to do anything in that war itself <\s>
<s> not of course that he had not supported the war from its inception with all his soul but between that and supporting it with the bodies of his wife and daughter there had been a gap fixed by something old fashioned within him which abhorred emotional extravagance <\s>
<s> he had for instance strongly objected to annette so attractive and in 1914 only thirty four going to her native france her chere patrie as under the stimulus of war she had begun to call it to nurse her braves poilus forsooth <\s>
<s> ruining her health and her looks <\s>
<s> as if she were really a nurse <\s>
<s> he had put a stopper on it <\s>
<s> let her do needlework for them at home or knit <\s>
<s> she had not gone therefore and had never been quite the same woman since <\s>
<s> a bad tendency of hers to mock at him not openly but in continual little ways had grown <\s>
<s> as for fleur the war had resolved the vexed problem whether or not she should go to school <\s>
<s> she was better away from her mother in her war mood from the chance of air raids and the impetus to do extravagant things so he had placed her in a seminary as far west as had seemed to him compatible with excellence and had missed her horribly <\s>
<s> he had never regretted the somewhat outlandish name by which at her birth he had decided so suddenly to call her marked concession though it had been to the french <\s>
<s> a pretty name a pretty child <\s>
<s> but restless too restless and wilful <\s>
<s> knowing her power too over her father <\s>
<s> soames often reflected on the mistake it was to dote on his daughter <\s>
<s> to get old and dote <\s>
<s> he was getting on but he didn't feel it for fortunately perhaps considering annette's youth and good looks his second marriage had turned out a cool affair <\s>
<s> he had known but one real passion in his life for that first wife of his irene <\s>
<s> yes and that fellow his cousin jolyon who had gone off with her was looking very shaky they said <\s>
<s> no wonder at seventy two after twenty years of a third marriage <\s>
<s> soames paused a moment in his march to lean over the railings of the row <\s>
<s> a suitable spot for reminiscence half way between that house in park lane which had seen his birth and his parents deaths and the little house in montpellier square where thirty five years ago he had enjoyed his first edition of matrimony <\s>
<s> now after twenty years of his second edition that old tragedy seemed to him like a previous existence which had ended when fleur was born in place of the son he had hoped for <\s>
<s> for many years he had ceased regretting even vaguely the son who had not been born fleur filled the bill in his heart <\s>
<s> after all she bore his name and he was not looking forward at all to the time when she would change it <\s>
<s> indeed if he ever thought of such a calamity it was seasoned by the vague feeling that he could make her rich enough to purchase perhaps and extinguish the name of the fellow who married her why not since as it seemed women were equal to men nowadays <\s>
<s> and soames secretly convinced that they were not passed his curved hand over his face vigorously till it reached the comfort of his chin <\s>
<s> thanks to abstemious habits he had not grown fat and gabby his nose was pale and thin his grey moustache close clipped his eyesight unimpaired <\s>
<s> a slight stoop closened and corrected the expansion given to his face by the heightening of his forehead in the recession of his grey hair <\s>
<s> little change had time wrought in the warmest of the young forsytes as the last of the old forsytes timothy now in his hundred and first year would have phrased it <\s>
<s> the shade from the plane trees fell on his neat homburg hat he had given up top hats it was no use attracting attention to wealth in days like these <\s>
<s> his thoughts travelled sharply to madrid the easter before the war when having to make up his mind about that goya picture he had taken a voyage of discovery to study the painter on his spot <\s>
<s> the fellow had impressed him great range real genius <\s>
<s> highly as the chap ranked he would rank even higher before they had finished with him <\s>
<s> the second goya craze would be greater even than the first oh yes <\s>
<s> and he had bought <\s>
